I'm writing to express my heartfelt gratitude to the employees of the midus store at 7340 blackstone ave in fresno. I cant thank the people there enough for what they did for me. They went so far above and beyond I cant even put into words how amazing they were. I needed to have my brakes fixed as another midus did not live up to the standards that have been set by the people at this store and I wanted new tires for my car. Which they were able to help me with. I had an appointment on the 7th of October at 9am, but the night of the 6th, my father went into the hospital and I was told I may only have a few hours left with him. I left the hospital at about 830 in the morning on the 7th so that other family could visit with him, and I could drop my car off. Hearing the situation, I was given a ride back to the hospital completely free of charge, and when my car was ready I was even given an uber back to the shop, where my car was ready and paperwork was ready to get me out of the store in less then 5 mins and to get me back to the hospital as fast as possible. My dad passed later on the night of the 7th.... while my heart is broken with loss, your team of employees, made it where I was able to hold my dads hand, and be there with him for every minute that he had left. I cant thank your team enough for what they did for me. While this has been one of the hardest points in my life, it has been the best from a service stand point. I just want to thank your entire team, I'm sorry I can't remember names right now, my mind is all over the place, it took a few days to even be able to form words, but I just want everyone to know how far the team went out of thier way for me and what they did for me. Also the work they did was great, the new tires and the brakes having them work again means a lot to my family as I am on the road a lot for work. I know I didnt say enough about your team as it is still hard to get my thoughts out lately, but I just wanted to say thank you, and I hope you are able to see how much it meant to me what they did. You have a customer for life, thank you so much.

John Schriner<//text>

< Review>
I would give this 10-stars if I could. Magical place to take a walk and enjoy the moments. You enter into a redwood forest with picnic tables and seating, and as you walk further it takes you along a perfect trail around a lake. The walking is flat and easy and the scenery is spectacular! On the walk I saw an egret, horses, and bald eagle. Also it seemed every other person walking was with their dog - every kind of dog imaginable, it was like a free dog show! I took my dog as well and she LOVED trotting along the trails. When we got to the end we ate some sandwiches at the picnic tables while relaxing under a redwood tree. Parking is $7 which is great to support our local parks. It's easy to get here. A true hidden gem!</Review>

< rating>
5</rating>
< text>
I love this park! The huge redwood trees at the entrance are gorgeous, with a great picnic area for large groups under their canopy. The trail around the lakes is wide and easy most of the way, until you get to the rocky area between the lakes that requires some scrambling when the water level is high. Nice spot for lake fishing, or head to the Russian River on the edge of the park. Fun trail along the edge of the lake with nice shady spots for relaxing with a good book or picnic. Some years I've seen the egret's nesting and heard the squawks of the chicks high in the trees - it's quite a sight! Great for a peaceful solo hike to enjoy the quiet and beauty, or for families to explore among the trees and catch a fish. And it's only 15 min north of Santa Rosa, right outside of quaint Windsor.</text>

<review>Riverfront Regional Park is a Sonoma County Park. You must have a park pass to use park or pay at gate. Not sure what fee is this yr though. I love it because it's an appx 3 mile loop around a beautiful lake. Its a nature trail and. Trail meanders through coastal redwoods, wildflowers, wildlife, birds. There are benches along the way if you need a rest. Restrooms are in the picnic area, set off a bit and the picnic area is centered under a most beautiful grovevof Coast Redwoods. There are other trails too. One is a steep climb. I attempted, but did not finish..(bad knee at time). But seasoned hikers will enjoy. There is no swimming in lake but non motorized boats and fishing are allowed. This park also sits adjacent to the Russian River and There is access to the water though I don't recall seeing much beach. You CAN swim in the river, though it's quite a hike from parking to water. Dogs on leash allowed too and poopy bags are provided as well. Peoples of all ages will enjoy something about this park.</review>< Pictures>

< Text>
Burlington isn't my cup of tea. Things are, for the most part, "discounted," but it's not spectacular and nothing you wouldn't find in sale prices at JCPenny, IMO. The Men's Big & Tall section was ok, but much of it you can find on sale at other stores and/or the brands tend to be knockoffs. The store feels kinda ghetto, and I don't throw that around often. I went there for a wallet, found one I liked that wasn't overly expensive, and that was that. Will I go back? Probably not. That's not a knock on the store, it's just not my kind of store.< /Text>

< Review>
I've been gaming with a group of buddies here on Tuesday nights for around a decade. The staff is friendly, the floors and bathrooms clean, the food competent; I do the all you can eat pizza and salad bar, and there's plenty of options (even for a vegetarian). There's even a 4 seat bar, so if we want a beer, we can grab a cold one. There's also a couple of different TVs that we can usually get turned off if we want, though they're not loud enough to be objectionable either (we watched the news on election night 2016 while we gamed). It's a Round Table in a strip mall, what else can I say?< /Review>

I'm sharing this because I know most people do not know much about auto maintenance/repair and are always at the mercy of the shops they visit.
For over two decades, I have been having oil changes for all my family's cars at the La Paz Jiffy Lube location with no problems.  I went there yesterday for an oil change and they first tried to sell me synthetic, while my car's manufacturer recommends regular oil ($50 more for synthetic).  They insisted that the manufacturer is not right, and they go by their own book. When I declined they got upset and became visibly rude.  Then they drained the oil for less than 10 seconds, and all of a sudden, they began filling the oil. When I questioned if they allowed all the oil to drain and if they changed the filter, they became furious and told me they do not need my business. They got upset because they were caught. When I got home, I checked the oil and it was not fully clean and the oil filter had not been changed.  I am warning all my neighbors not to go to this location, as they will surely be scammed.  They could not do that to me because I was a mechanic many years ago and I know how things work around cars and garages. I have reported them to the Consumer Affairs-Department of Automotive Repair.  If you have had a scam experience with them or any other garage, you should take a couple of minutes to file a complaint.</review>

< review>
We‚Äôve been coming here many, many times, usually as a group of 6 to 8 people.  The second Chinese character in the restaurant‚Äôs name means Hunan.  Hunan region is famous for their spicy and heavily flavored food.  You can find some dishes that are not spicy but then you‚Äôd miss the main reason the customers come to eat here.  Service is always quick and attentive.  Food, well, is very spicy, even if you ask them for not-so-spicy for the dish.  The price is very reasonable.  This is my place to go for spicy Hunan food.  This time, we arrived at 5:45 on a Sunday evening and were able to get a table right away.  By the time we were done, 7:20 PM, it was crowded with around 20 to 30 people outside waiting to be seated.<//review>

<review>They were open for Christmas night.

Family ordered their share of food, and I ordered the baked shrimps and sizzling beef.

< Review>
It was our first time to Ping's Bistro.
Service & ambience, I give it 4 Stars.
Food, I give it 2.5 Stars.
Wait Time, I give it 2.5 Stars.
Prices, 2.5 Stars ($75 for 3pp).
We came based on the reviews & for the Steamed Fish Filet w/Peppers (similar to Dual Fish we liked at Shao Mountain restaurant that closed).  The waiting area in front only had room to seat 4pp & was pretty cramp for the 3 of us standing along w/2 others.  We arrived at 8pm on a Sat night & our table for 3pp got seated in 30mins.  The seats at our table were comfortable but the spot light above was a bit too glaring.  Service was ok.  Our food came pretty fast & portions were big.  Our $12 large milktea was big enough for the 3 of us to split & have 1.5 cups each.  Unfortunately, the milktea was the only item we really liked.  The Shredded Chicken Noodle w/Cucumbers was not spicy nor flavorful enough.  The Chairman Mao's Braised Pork Belly was ok, but not tender enough.  We were really disappointed with the Steamed Fish Filet w/Peppers;  It was extremely salty & not spicy enough also.  We tried to scrape off the green & red peppers sauce on top to see if it would be better but it was still too salty to eat.  I brought the leftovers home & my boyfriend tried the Chairman Mao's Braised Pork Belly & said it sucked because it wasn't tender & kind of dry.
We probably won't be back.</Review>
